< review>
What can I say? Authentic Mexican food at either low or reasonable prices. The wet burrito's great, my brother would definitely recommend their burgers, and my mom really likes their specialty weekend soups. Even their non-Mexican dishes, like their fish dinner, surpasses usual restaurant quality. I'm trying to think of something wrong with it, but I simply can't. Thanks, Vega's, you honestly made last Sunday a whole lot better.
Edit: Oh, yeah, I forgot to mention that everyone was wearing a mask. Not only does this place serve some good food, but they care about your safety, too.</review>

< Text>
I love OTF to the point of near addiction which is saying a lot coming from a 20yr fitness hiatus. I travel a lot of work and have been to Orange Theory studios across the country. The Santa Monica coaches are the best I've seen. They are great motivators and knowledgeable technique-focused trainers. They meet you where you're at in your fitness journey and never make you feel bad about things you can't yet do. You'll see a mix of fitness levels in class which you'll find refreshing. The vibe is supportive, friendly and not competitive. Definitely check out Rusty's classes. His coaching keeps you accountable and motivated, his music is great, and his humor keeps the mood light.</Text>

This is review is on 1/5/2021. You should re-consider joining this YMCA to use the swimming pool.  With their new policy for reservations you will not be able to book a lane a week in advance, you will need to be put onto a wait list and might or might not be use the swimming poll when you get them.  I had spoke to the staff there about my concern, while they recognized my concerns they are not going to do anything to the reservations, even when I ask them if members can rotate their swimming reservations.  I have been swimming there almost 5 days (morning) a week.  When I was able to swim there the lanes are not full, people not showing up, so the system is not helping the actual swimmers but people who might able to occupy the reservation but not to show up.

In case the swim department decided to address this "bottle neck" of their swimming pool there will be too many people trying to book the lane and not show up, than actual swimmers that would be able to use the swimming pool.

Look for another pool!</text>

<time>1355001681126<//time>< text>
The Scheu Family YMCA is a fantastic place for families of all ages.  I've been a member for almost 2-years and love it.

The facility offers:
* indoor soccer arena
* basketball court/gymnasium - 6 hoops
* free weights
* circuit machine weights
* treadmills
* stair stepper
* elliptical trainers
* exercise bikes including recumbent bikes

In addition this facility has:
* bike spinning room
* dance room
* pool table
* table tennis (ping pong)
* cardiac room
* young kids play area

Classes are numerous for both kids and adults.  For adults the most popular classes include pilates, Zumba, and cardio.

NOTE: This facility was the former Wayne Gretzky roller hockey park and converted into a YMCA.  The roller hockey field is now an indoor soccer area.< /text>

<UserId.>103896613243697491714< /UserId.><Rating>2</Rating>< Text>
This is as honest a post as I can make. I don‚Äôt like giving negative reviews but in this case I feel it‚Äôs justified. I‚Äôm giving 2 stars not 1 because I think 1 star reviews are rarely taken seriously and seem more like disgruntled people who want to sink a business rather than give the public a heads-up. Berco was actually referred to us by a friend who had a positive experience. I will post pictures here on google of all the issues I describe below. I am also ignorant to the industry lingo and technical terms so I‚Äôll describe things in layman‚Äôs terms.
Went to the store/showroom to describe the redwood fence project and look we wanted. The staff was very helpful and recommended a product that consisted of (measurements are approximate for this review as I can‚Äôt recall the exact measurements given to us) an 8-foot long, 3-inch thick board sanded/finished smooth on both sides that is then cut/milled longways in half so when it comes out the other side you have two 8-for long boards 1-1/2‚Äù thick, with one side on each board being smooth and the other side being rough. The boards then get run through a type of router or something that bevels or rounds the edges for a nice smooth rounded edge on the smooth side. The smooth side is then supposed to be the side showing with the opposite rough side as the side facing the fence posts. We ordered over 70 boards for our project and the cost was over $2500.
When the product was delivered and I started to unload the boards from their pallet, I noticed that the cuts were uneven. For example, some boards were 2‚Äù thick, while it‚Äôs counterpart was only 1‚Äù thick. Some boards were damaged, some boards were 7-1/2‚Äù wide, some were 7-1/4‚Äù wide, some were 7-3/4‚Äù wide. Lots of the boards had what looked to be material/wood chewed off the one end that was inserted into the mill; I can only assume this was the same carelessness that uneven measurements and different sized boards came from. I called Berco and they were very apologetic and understanding of our concerns, and said to separate the boards that we didn‚Äôt want and they would send a truck to pick up those ones and bring replacements. The manager then called me back later that day and said he was going to personally go into the yard and hand-pick all new boards and replace the entire load. Needless to say I was impressed with the customer service. But when the new load came, and I was unloading it, the same issues were evident in the first load. I proceeded to use the boards because the project had already taken a delay due to the replacement of the first load and I needed to get the fence built before my neighbor came back from vacation due to her dogs needing her backyard.
The fence is done and looks good from far away, but if you get close you can see the imperfections in the boards, especially where the boards meet on the posts. Granted, some may say ‚Äúit‚Äôs just a fence, what do you want?‚Äù or maybe I‚Äôm making too much of a stink over a fence, but if it was just a fence I could have built one using lumber/boards from a big box store and gotten the job done for a fraction of the price. We wanted a higher-end looking fence using higher end products. Unfortunately Berco supplied an inferior product not once but twice, and even after saying they‚Äôd make it right. Very disappointed and will be going elsewhere for the lumber for the back and opposite side fence Instill need to build. See pictures.</Text>

The course is laid out amongst beautiful trees, along a creek, and setup around some fields. You are welcome to walk through the area, just be aware of very fast-moving frisbees flying around. There is also 2 playgrounds, including one for toddlers. But the star of this park is the frisbee course.< /review>
